  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_66c5ca43-90b9-45f8-9d14-f9f957d74269'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText10882320883695704294" style="display:none">Book 7 in the New Species series. <br /><br />Zandy's had too much to drink and is in the wrong place at the wrong time. She knows she's going to die. When next her eyes open, a beautiful man-creature is holding her in his arms. He's just too tempting to resist; her very own fallen angel. She wraps herself around his body, determined to have him. But when this angel turns out to be flesh and blood, reality crashes in-she's seducing a New Species. <br /><br />Tiger's shock quickly turns to intense passion when the human female kisses him, despite the fact she's trying to get his clothes off while he's engaged in a task force operation. He's also made it clear he'll never take a mate. Rather difficult when he and Zandy can't keep their hands off each other. The taste and feel of his little human just leaves Tiger wanting more.<br /><br /> Publisher's Note: While each New Species book is a standalone, the greatest enjoyment will come from reading them in series order.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1213250643" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer615235757236377679"><b>4.5 tempting tiger Stars</b><br/><br/><b>*Spoilers*</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/MyGodThatsAmazing_zpszazhq7jb.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425146746ra/13853413.gif' alt=' photo MyGodThatsAmazing_zpszazhq7jb.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>“Drained,” he rasped. “You take it all from me. I feel almost turned inside out.”</b><br/><br/>Tiger is the 7th book in the New Species Series. Tiger doesn't want a mate ever.... He makes fun of all the males that have taken mates, saying they are nothing but trouble especially human mates. He has been very outspoken on the matter! Tiger is the head of security for the NSO, he and his men are called to break up a brawl at a local bar. When they arrive he sees this little </span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11315694627573340109">Well, we are back to a lot of angst, but it was still really good. There is a ton of humor in these books because of the bluntness of the New Species. They just say exactly what they mean, in a literal way, that is sometimes shocking, but always funny.<br/><br/>In this book we have Zandy and Tiger. Tiger has always been a great character throughout the series. He has been level-headed and humorous, but definitely against being with human women. He makes fun of those who fall for them.... until it happens </span>
  <span id="freeText11315694627573340109" style="display:none">Well, we are back to a lot of angst, but it was still really good. There is a ton of humor in these books because of the bluntness of the New Species. They just say exactly what they mean, in a literal way, that is sometimes shocking, but always funny.<br><br>In this book we have Zandy and Tiger. Tiger has always been a great character throughout the series. He has been level-headed and humorous, but definitely against being with human women. He makes fun of those who fall for them.... until it happens to him.<br><br><b>
  <i>What is wrong with me? He wasn't sure but the desire to tend her was strong. A Species female would have hit him by now and never allowed him to coddle her in any way. Zandy stepped closer...<br><br>The fact that she was submissive to him without him having to display aggression during sex left him reeling.<br><br>No, she's not anything like a Species. This is how it starts, he realized. Those poor males who ended up with human mates had to have felt what he did. Protective. Possessive.</i>
</b><br><br>Yeah, it turns out that the New Species females will wrestle the males before submitting to sex. That sounds like fun - not! If I had to wrestle my hubs every time he wanted sex, he wouldn't be getting sex. I don't even go to the gym. I hate having to walk up stairs. I park in parking spots as close to the stores as I can get. There ain't no way I'm wrestling my giant husband at night.<br><br>So, Zandy (and, let's not get into why she's named Zandy. Someone was running out of name ideas, me thinks.) starts working at the New Species compound and her job is to work with another human answering mail. The New Species get giant bags of hate mail each day. Much like Donald Trump. Except, his is deserved. (That reminds me, I need to write a letter...)<br><br>Tiger wants Zandy, but doesn't. Zandy has been married and divorced twice, so she's not exactly in a rush for lucky number three. So, in comes the angst.<br><br>And, guess who else shows up in this book? Our New Species guy from the last one, Vengeance von Rapist. Yeah, the one who tried to rape whatever-her-name-was in the last book shows up to do a smash-and-grab on Zandy. <br><br>So, Tiger goes out to his house to kick his ass, and damn it if they didn't somehow make me feel sorry for Mr. Von Rapist! He's just an idiot who wants a mate so badly that he thinks if he catches one, he can convince her to love him. How wrong can you be, Mr. Von Rapist? Women in books <b>never</b> fall in love with their kidnappers!<br><br><b>
  <i>"I'm so lonely and I would be an excellent mate."<br><br>Tiger stalked closer.."You can't just carry one off. It would be cool if it was that easy but it's not."<br><br>"I'm skilled at sharing sex and I have learned how to cook. I'm an excellent fighter. I would keep her warm in my arms and die to protect her."</i>
</b><br><br>Awww, let's give him something!<br><br>So, now I'm hoping Mr. Von Rapist will get a mate. I hate things to be lonely. I can't even stand for my salt and pepper shakers to be separated for very long. They belong together, people!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457560997i/18375138._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Huh, I think I need this... I'm off to shop now. See you guys later. :)</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5308757275676675905">4.75/5<br/><br/>Absolutely fantastic!<br/><br/>To be honest, I didn't expect much from this book considering the previous installments in this series were really hit and miss for me, but it was actually a real surprise. I didn't expect that it would give me so much pleasure and that I would end up loving it, but I just simply did. I loved it. I loved almost everything about this book!<br/><br/>Despite the fact that the books in this series have all been formulaic to such an extent, and this one contains some of the same elem</span>
  <span id="freeText5308757275676675905" style="display:none">4.75/5<br /><br />Absolutely fantastic!<br /><br />To be honest, I didn't expect much from this book considering the previous installments in this series were really hit and miss for me, but it was actually a real surprise. I didn't expect that it would give me so much pleasure and that I would end up loving it, but I just simply did. I loved it. I loved almost everything about this book!<br /><br />Despite the fact that the books in this series have all been formulaic to such an extent, and this one contains some of the same elements as the others, I really did enjoy it and speedily turned the pages, anticipating what would happen next.<br /><br />Normally, when I read the previous books in this series, I had to skim over boring filler and I always felt like the stories were overly long. But I can’t believe there was never a dull moment in this one! It was beyond enjoyable!<br /><br />The story started off very well. Tiger saved Zandy's life when she was at the bar. She was drunk and thought she was going to die. When she opened her eyes and saw Tiger, she thought he was an angel. She kissed him and they almost had sex on the hood of the Jeep, but then the ambulance arrived. Both of them never thought that their paths would cross again. Later, Zandy was fired because she refused to sleep with her boss, but she got a new job at the NSO where they bumped into each other again. The sparks between them reignited immediately and they couldn't resist the attraction toward each other.<br /><br />After two divorces, Zandy didn’t believe in marriage no more, while Tiger never wanted a mate, especially female human mate, so they agreed to continue seeing each other for sex only. However, as they spent more and more time together, their feelings grew stronger, deeper, and more intense. Finally, Tiger stopped fighting his desires to claim her as his, but first thing first, he had to prove to her that he was a trustworthy mate.<br /><br /><br /><i>
  <b>“You’re mine, Zandy. You have been since the moment you woke up on the hood of that Jeep and kissed me. I just didn’t want to admit it at first but you’re my mate and I’m yours.”</b>
</i><br /><br /><br />I loved both Tiger and Zandy. Tiger is amazing and Zanday is kick-ass. I admired her stoicism and her bravery. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[When she was kidnapped from her house and taken to an old motor home, although she was hurt and so scared, she tried not to show it. Instead of crying and begging her captors to let her go, she kept insulting and provoking them with mocking words. Damn, that was priceless! And I was like—you go girl, make them regret they were ever born! Why not? These crazy morons were going to burn her alive! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I couldn’t help but smile from ear to ear as I read the epilogue. It was wonderful! Without a doubt, this is the best installment in New Species series so far.<br /><br />Couldn’t be happier! Loved it!<br /><br /><br />-------------------------------------------<br /><br /><br /><b>**BR with my lovely friends, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1519885980?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Aileene</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1599062903?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Jess</a>.</b><br /></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1599062903" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer12184690187786357261"><b>All aboard the mind-crack train!</b> It's back on the rails and I love this book even with all of the stupid shit that happens along the way. <br/><br/>I don't know why, but I don't think Laurann Dohner ever actually learnt how to structure a story properly. I'm yet to read a NS book that actually flows. They always go wildly from sex to drama, to unplanned pregnancy/kidnapping/other miscellaneous and unecessary dramatics, to happy ending. But I'm letting it slide because this one <u>gave me butterflies</u>!<br/><br/>While th</span>
  <span id="freeText12184690187786357261" style="display:none"><b>All aboard the mind-crack train!</b> It's back on the rails and I love this book even with all of the stupid shit that happens along the way. <br><br>I don't know why, but I don't think Laurann Dohner ever actually learnt how to structure a story properly. I'm yet to read a NS book that actually flows. They always go wildly from sex to drama, to unplanned pregnancy/kidnapping/other miscellaneous and unecessary dramatics, to happy ending. But I'm letting it slide because this one <u>gave me butterflies</u>!<br><br>While this was enjoyable and I looked forward to being able to read it, it did have issues that I couldn't look past, for example:<br><br>I'm totally not down with Tiger trying to impregnate Zandy without her knowledge or consent. Like, dude. <u>Come on</u>. <i>HOWEVER</i> I did get an amazing Alexa Riley vibe from the whole <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ "I need to bind you to me so you won't leave me"  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> thing that happened at the end there.<br><br>For the head of security, Tiger sure isn't very careful about the security of Zandy. The number of times she gets into trouble in this is ridiculous. <br><br>And how many times do I need to say this, guys? <b>Communication</b> is what is needed for a successful relationship. If you two had have been up front about your feelings from the beginning, you could have saved yourself a lot of trouble.<br><br>The best bit about this book, was Zandy. <b>HOORAY for a female who won't take any shit from the leading man</b>. When Tiger rips into her after she is attacked, she tells him to get his head out of his ass and that she will <u>not be blamed for being a victim</u>. Then she locks him out of her apartment for being such a dick! A++++++++++ Zandy. Love you! You go girlfriend!<br><br>So. Even though I had problems with this, the sex was off the charts, Tiger was a babe (when he wasn't being an idiot) and Zandy was amazing. <br><br>I want Smiley's book ASAP but I understand that I have to get through a bunch of other ones first, but I'm no longer dreading the rest of this series like I was a few books ago. <br><br>Bring on the next book!<br><br><b>4</b> <i>sploosh-train</i> <b>Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481163842i/21393092.png" alt="Mountain View" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481163842i/21393092.png" alt="Mountain View" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481163842i/21393092.png" alt="Mountain View" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Thank you for the buddy read, my fellow New Species lovers <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1519885980" rel="nofollow noopener">Aileene</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1820494451" rel="nofollow noopener">Alp</a>! :)</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

</blockquote> Oh my…..this is me when I was reading this book………………<blockquote>

</blockquote><br>Tiger’s story….have been so looking forward to it. The gorgeous tiger/male species….swoon…<blockquote>&lt;=”<a href="http://s1290.photobucket.com/user/dasilvazak/media/writing%20inspirations%209/efaf861b3dfa0b35848cadc3a7d10010_zps2dc4b3c9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397304871i/9260742.jpg" alt=" photo efaf861b3dfa0b35848cadc3a7d10010_zps2dc4b3c9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote> He’s been such a “strutter” in the previous books….and now we get to see him not only roaring but purring too….<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397304871i/9260741.jpg" alt=" photo images5_zpsf56b58ab.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>especially when Zandy is near him.<br><br>I loved the beginning of this book when Tiger first meets Zandy. Absolutely hilarious.<br>So, we all know the plot – species meets human female, who falls in love immediately with him…I can understand that…these are gorgeous species!!! Lots of scenting, sniffing, mounting around…..in fact there were so many sex scenes – now don’t get me wrong…I like those…but after one and then another a few pages later and then yet another….and so on…I started skipping those couplings….after all, how much can I read over and over again about licking, you taste so sweet, ooh you are so big – it kind of became a bit repetitive….you know what I am trying to say!!!!<br><br>Zandy….well at first I had this idea…what a slut!!!! But, no, she’s actually quite a likeable character and I enjoyed the way she drove Tiger crazy…what’s a girl got to do if the guy is acting like an idiot and can’t see the jewel in front of his eyes!!!!<br><br>Love the secondary characters – Creek, Smiley, Moon, Harley and the sad and broken Vengeance. <br>What an amazing world this author has created…and never mind if it’s far-fetched, that some of the dialogue is totally wacky, that there is so much repetitive sex scenes…….it matters not…because I get such enjoyment and entertainment reading this series.<br>Some quotes I liked - <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397304871i/9260743._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo d32b1d1f41116e33e977eb96ecec7bb3_zps0d7f7ef7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br> <a href="http://s1290.photobucket.com/user/dasilvazak/media/writing%20inspirations%209/6e2e625ce926df23888663848396279a_zps4fa3fe27.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397304871i/9260744._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 6e2e625ce926df23888663848396279a_zps4fa3fe27.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>So, leaving Tiger and Zandy with their HEA and may they continue doing much of this TOGETHER…….<blockquote>
<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397306029i/9260904.jpg" alt=" photo images1_zpsed7876f2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh...yes, yes...love this cover!!!!!</blockquote></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer295611777" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5812120829425043514"> Somebody once told me to start reading the ‘New Species’ series if I liked any of the Lora Leigh ‘Breed’ books….<br/>Thus, I started reading the New species ebooks, and promptly decided to throw away all the Breed books. :)<br/>The premises is the same, but the way Laurann Dohner builds up her world? Well it rocks MY world.<br/>I am completely in love with all of her books-still, ‘Tiger’ is now firmly on <b>favorites</b> shelf.<br/><br/>Why?<br/><br/>Well,we have met the anti-species protestors and terrorist in the previous books. Dram</span>
  <span id="freeText5812120829425043514" style="display:none"> Somebody once told me to start reading the ‘New Species’ series if I liked any of the Lora Leigh ‘Breed’ books….<br />Thus, I started reading the New species ebooks, and promptly decided to throw away all the Breed books. :)<br />The premises is the same, but the way Laurann Dohner builds up her world? Well it rocks MY world.<br />I am completely in love with all of her books-still, ‘Tiger’ is now firmly on <b>favorites</b> shelf.<br /><br />Why?<br /><br />Well,we have met the anti-species protestors and terrorist in the previous books. Drama, terror and prejudice, just the way I like it! Everything was peachy!<br />But there was this one part that blew me away…<br /><br />I got so involved I could almost taste the fear when my heroine was captured by the protestors…there I was,biting my nails…and then this happened…<br /><br /><br /><i>The bench was eased to the ground and the two large men unfastened her restraints. She’d been flat for so long that she felt a little dizzy<br />when she sat up. The older woman approached, looking fearful.<br />“Now, don’t you spin your head at me or anything.”<br />Zandy’s smart mouth kicked in. “I think you watched way too many horror movies. I’m not possessed.”<br />The woman frowned. “Do you need to go pee-pee?”<br />Pee-pee? Really? Just bitchin’. I’ve been kidnapped by idiots who use a two-year-old’s vocabulary. “Yes.”<br />They didn’t remove the handcuffs which held her wrists locked in front of her. The woman gripped them in the middle and led Zandy over<br />to one of the campers, tugging on the chain as if she were leading a dog.<br />“Don’t try anything evil,” Deanie warned. “I’m watching you.”<br />Zandy’s gaze swept the interior, looking for a weapon but the place was pretty bare. Dishes had all been put away and the woman refused<br />to release the chain on the restraints. The bathroom was a tiny one.<br />“Go ahead. You hurry up.” Her voice lowered. “Stop giving my son grief, young lady. You’re trying to make him look bad in front of his<br />followers. Do you know how hard it was for him to gather so many of them?”<br />It was a struggle to get her pants undone and use the bathroom with her hands locked together. “No. Not really. I haven’t read much<br />about cults.”<br />Deanie gasped. “Shame on you for even saying that. We’re—” The woman glanced down and gasped a second time. “Sinner! I see that<br />whore’s underwear instead of what should be decent covering for your private area. Tsk, tsk! No wonder you were lured to the dark side.”<br />Zandy blinked a few times. “They had really good cookies and they approved of thong underwear. What can I say? I didn’t stand a<br />chance.”<br />Her sarcasm was totally lost on her captor as Deanie frowned. “What does that mean? What kind of cookies?”<br />“Oh geez. You people are seriously screwed up. No wonder your kid is so messed up.”<br />“You’re an evil sinner with a potty mouth. Shame on you.” She turned around and jerked open a drawer built into the wall. She turned,<br />holding out bright blue shorts. “Remove that whore garment and put this on.”<br />“Are those swimming trunks?”<br />“Yes.”<br />“No.”<br />“You will. You can’t cleanse your soul when you’re wearing that bright-red sin tempter. We’re trying to save you, not send you to hell.”<br />“I’m already there, lady.”<br />Deanie’s face reddened. “Change or I’ll have the men come in here to do it for you. These are clean and pure.”<br />The thought of Adam or those other creeps taking her pants off made Zandy decide to comply. The men’s swimming trunks were a bit<br />big but it seemed to have soothed the upset woman when she almost smiled.<br />“Much better.”<br />The irony wasn’t lost on her. They were going to burn her to death wearing swimming trunks. </i><br /><br />….I laughed my head off. And this is what makes a good author…great suspense, AND humor. Mrs. Dohner made the perfect blend. She should sell the recipe to other writer out there-she would make a fortune! Add in the steamy sex, wonderful romance, and good character development and you have an all around winner!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5812120829425043514" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

              <span id="reviewTextContainer262039669" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer8405456675934217072">5.0 Stars!<br/><br/>This get's five stars not because the story is so intricate and imaginative or because the emotion sucked me in and made me cry. But because it was such a great story.<br/><br/>I love these New Species folks and I was enthralled from page one...this novel had plenty of action, excitement and just kept a steady pace right to the end.<br/><br/>Sex is smoken, Tiger is funny, love Vengeance....poor Veng...someone find him a human woman! One of the funniest and saddest scenes is where Tiger is telling Vengeanc</span>
  <span id="freeText8405456675934217072" style="display:none">5.0 Stars!<br /><br />This get's five stars not because the story is so intricate and imaginative or because the emotion sucked me in and made me cry. But because it was such a great story.<br /><br />I love these New Species folks and I was enthralled from page one...this novel had plenty of action, excitement and just kept a steady pace right to the end.<br /><br />Sex is smoken, Tiger is funny, love Vengeance....poor Veng...someone find him a human woman! One of the funniest and saddest scenes is where Tiger is telling Vengeance he can't go all cave man on human women and he is trying to explain to him how to whoo a woman....but he just doesn't get it and breaks down in tears (from a new species male) because he misses his mate and wants a new one. He is lonely. Along with Veng we got to get to know some of the secondary characters from previous books a little better in this novel.<br /><br />It was romantic, sweet at times, wonderfully balanced between the excitement and the softer, intimate times. I loved these two together, they really seemed to be so well suited. Our boy Tiger bit the bullet and has a baby on the way....This is so funny considering he spent the entire first 7 books making fun of his friends who found their mate and swore off mating to a female himself.....I can only wonder who is next?</span>

<div id="review_314795810" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/314795810" />
    <a title="Adria&#39;s Musings" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5832861-adria-s-musings"><img alt="Adria&#39;s Musings" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1593543967p2/5832861.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/314795810?book_show_action=true">Apr 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Adria&#39;s Musings" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Adria&#39;s Musings" href="/user/show/5832861-adria-s-musings">Adria&#39;s Musings</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5832861-adria-s-musings?shelf=read-and-reviewed">read-and-reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer314795810" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14871005369648232839">Sigh, Tiger, Tiger, Tiger. What can I say? I've been waiting to read about Tiger since I first met him in Fury. He was smart, funny, charming and hell bent on NOT taking a mate. Throughout the New Species series, Tiger became more and more sure that he would never take a mate, especially a human one. So I knew that the woman he fell in love with would have to be unique and a little on the crazy side to take on Tiger.<br/><br/>Enter Zandy Gordon. Goodness even her name is unique. It took some getting used </span>
  <span id="freeText14871005369648232839" style="display:none">Sigh, Tiger, Tiger, Tiger. What can I say? I've been waiting to read about Tiger since I first met him in Fury. He was smart, funny, charming and hell bent on NOT taking a mate. Throughout the New Species series, Tiger became more and more sure that he would never take a mate, especially a human one. So I knew that the woman he fell in love with would have to be unique and a little on the crazy side to take on Tiger.<br /><br />Enter Zandy Gordon. Goodness even her name is unique. It took some getting used to her name since it's the first time I've ever met a character with that name, but she's definitely one of a kind. When the reader first meets Zandy, she's a little down on her luck, she refuses to sleep with her boss and he's making her life hell, so she decided to drown her sorrows at Mickey's Bar and Grill. Big mistake. A bar fight breaks out and Zandy's caught in the middle! She soon finds herself being crushed under the weight of some of the fighting patrons and believes she's going to die. Until help arrives.<br /><br />Tiger and his NSO team have been called upon by the local sheriff to help break up the bar fight. Once Tiger realizes that under a bunch of drunken bodies, is a human female his protective instincts kick in. He literally throws the bodies off of the Zandy until he gets to her. Once he frees her however, she isn't breathing. After administering CPR, Tiger carries Zandy outside, where she believes she's died and Tiger has come to escort her to hell. Thinking she has nothing left to lose, she practically molests him in public! The whole scene should be amusing but instead it's hot, really, really hot.<br /><br />Fast forward a few weeks and Zandy's been fired from her job and is waiting to be interviewed for a new one, with the New Species. She gets the job at the incoming mail department, sorting through fan mail, hate mail and threats. Hoping she doesn't run into Tiger, she heads to lunch and just when she thinks luck is on her side, in walks Tiger and he looks just as good as she remembers.<br /><br />The two begin what they foolishly think is a sex only relationship and it is rather entertaining to watch these two become more emotionally involved. Especially Tiger. He's in denial throughout most of the book, it's kind of like watching someone with an addiction. He refuses to admit he's got a problem. It's more of a pride thing really, he's been so adamant about not wanting to take a mate, especially a human and has given his mated friends such grief that he knows any interaction/relationship with Zandy is bound to bite him in the ass if it is made public.<br /><br />At the same time, things heat up in a bad way for the New Species, news of their leader and public figure Justice North's mating and marriage to a human woman (Book 4, Justice) has people in a frenzy, especially the hate groups, who mistake Zandy for Justice's mate, Jessie. After an attack outside of the gates of Reservation, Zandy is forced to stay in the human housing within the gates where she is attacked yet again by a human intruder (This poor woman really can't catch a break). You might be thinking, "She sounds like one of those wimpy female characters that's always in trouble and the male has to always save her to prove how macho he is."<br /><br />Well you couldn't be more wrong.<br /><br />Zandy's a strong female character but because she's human and is New Species friendly, that just makes her a really easy target for the Anti-New Species groups in the book. Each attack on Zandy also serves to bring Tiger closer to accepting the fact that he has it bad for her, that he's falling in love with her and that if he keeps fighting it, one day he might just lose her to the hate groups and he will have never told her or shown her how he felt and how good it could be between them. Added to the life threatening attacks is the fact that there's another New Species male interested in Zandy. Tiger doesn't have much time to make up his mind on whether he wants to keep the no-strings attached relationship with Zandy, or take the chance and see if he and Zandy could have something more precious together.<br /><br />What I love about the New Species males, besides them being really tall, buff and well, talented in the bedroom is their frankness. They don't bullshit you, they tell you how it is and sometimes it comes out wrong, you have to remember that they were locked up and denied basic interaction that didn't pertain to experimentation. They can be funny without trying, because they have animal instincts and behaviors that while natural in the wild, are a bit strange and mortifying coming from a man, as Zandy finds out constantly.<br /><br /><a href="http://romance-haven.blogspot.com/2012/04/review-tiger-by-laurann-dohner.html" rel="nofollow noopener">MORE HERE</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="14871005369648232839" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Laurann Dohner fans, shifter fans</span></div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer280168895" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8466720207767587704">I'm on the verge between "it was ok" and "I liked it" thus the 2.5 star rating. <br/><br/>Quick overview: Zandy (whose name I hated at first but then it grew on me) gets rescued by our New Species hero, Tiger, when she inadvertently finds herself in the middle of a bar brawl. He rescues her and she proceeds to feel him up on the bonnet of a car. <br/><br/>Fast forward a few weeks and Zandy finds herself in the position of needing a new job and she ends up scoring the position in the mail room at Reservation...one o</span>
  <span id="freeText8466720207767587704" style="display:none">I'm on the verge between "it was ok" and "I liked it" thus the 2.5 star rating. <br /><br />Quick overview: Zandy (whose name I hated at first but then it grew on me) gets rescued by our New Species hero, Tiger, when she inadvertently finds herself in the middle of a bar brawl. He rescues her and she proceeds to feel him up on the bonnet of a car. <br /><br />Fast forward a few weeks and Zandy finds herself in the position of needing a new job and she ends up scoring the position in the mail room at Reservation...one of the New Species bases. Obviously, she re-encounters Tiger and they pick up from where they left off on the bonnet and despite the fact that Tiger isn't all that keen on taking a mate, they have lots and lots and lots of sex. <br /><br />Throw in some action and kidnapping and we gots us a story people!<br /><br />&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;<b>SPOILERS AHEAD</b>&gt;&gt;&gt;&gt;&gt;&gt;&gt;&gt;&gt;&gt;&gt;<br /><br />What I liked:<br /><br />I liked Zandy and Tiger and I liked them together. It was good romance development and I didn't want to punch either of them like I did with Wrath and Lauren...so yeah. That was good.<br /><br />That one of the NS males <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[finally got hurt for once! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> At least it was something different!<br /><br />Good flow. Pacing didn't seem sluggish like it did with the last NS book.<br /><br />What I didn't like:<br /><br />The constant reference to Zandy's 'heat'.<b>WE GET IT</b> They can smell it when she's ovulating and when she's horny.<br /><br />Zandy sassing out the leader of the hate group. Don't get me wrong, I like that she shows spine, but it seemed unrealistic. If someone was planning to burn me alive I would be mute with fear and peeing my pants. I don't know maybe that's just me. Just seemed a bit unrealistic IMO.<br /><br />The inner monologue that the characters have drives me batty sometimes. Parts of it just seem so juvenile and stilted. This quote from Zandy really stood out for me. <br /><br /><i>"Was Tiger okay? Upset? She wouldn’t blame him if he hated humans. She just hoped he didn’t lump her in with the ones who’d attacked Homeland. Were the injured New Species friends of his? She stood and turned off the television. He’d call her and she’d ask him about it. She’d be there for him if he needed her. She put on her shoes and walked to the door, wanting to get to work."</i><br /><br />My overall impression: easy and relatively enjoyable paranormal read but I think, for me, the storyline is getting a bit stale. I'd love to see a switch up... New Species female with a human male! 2.5 stars :) <br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

  <span id="freeText5842836009155443108" style="display:none">I now have a new favorite in the NEW SPECIES series by Laurann Dohner.Loved this book,loved this couple together.Did I forget to mention how much I loved Tiger!I think that every girl deserves a Tiger in her life.I have to say that this was the most romantic of the New Species heros in every way.They meet when the heroine Zandy is almost crushed to death in a bar fight and Tiger rescues her,she has passed out due to being sufficated .He takes her outside and places her on the hood of his Jeep,she thinks that she has died and that Tiger is her "Angel".They share a verrry passionate kiss or should I say kisses before they are interupted.They next meet again at Reservation where Zandy now has a job working in their mailroom.Things heats up between this couple and the story moves along nicely.Of course there is the usual holding back by the Hero as he feels that he can not take a mate,esp,a human one at that.He has seen the dangers that a human mate has endured and he does not want that.This does not stop them from having sex,sex,and more sex.I loved the scene by the waterfall,so romantic.Of course, the heroine does get threats ,gets abducted and tied to a cross ,but our hero saves the day.I loved how Ms.Dohner has inc an epilogue as I do not believe she has done so before.All in all,a great read and can not wait for the next which I hope it will be soon.There was a very moving scene with Vengance when discussing his dead mate,my heart went out to him,so very lonley,I hope that he gets a heroine that is worthy of him.Will def be doing a reread on this soon.</span>

        rated it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer418348383" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8635846620100124150">First of all: If this book was the only one I had read in this serie(they can be read as stand alone books) I would have rated it higher. Tiger has been my favorite new species ever since he first got introduced and he doesn't disappoint in this book. Another great thing about this book is of course Vengeance. And I am pretty sure I am not the only reader wishing he would carry ME into the woods becauce I would not at all fight back. <br/><br/>When that's said, the reason behind my low rating is that I am</span>
  <span id="freeText8635846620100124150" style="display:none">First of all: If this book was the only one I had read in this serie(they can be read as stand alone books) I would have rated it higher. Tiger has been my favorite new species ever since he first got introduced and he doesn't disappoint in this book. Another great thing about this book is of course Vengeance. And I am pretty sure I am not the only reader wishing he would carry ME into the woods becauce I would not at all fight back. <br /><br />When that's said, the reason behind my low rating is that I am so sick of these books having the same build up, in _every_ book. The new species universe is wonderful, Dohner has created something I wish I was a part of. But the books by now, for me, are just average because they are all to alike!It's like I've read two species books instead of 7!<br /><br />When Dohner has created this amazing universe, why doesn't she expand the story? Why don't have two parallel stories in the books instead of having one major love drama and just some minor disturbances from hate groups on the side? Why introduce new species all the time instead of having a little more focus on the species we have grown to love? (Valiant? Where are you? Fury? Hello?) <br />Male meets female, male is possessive, female falls for male, female gets kidnapped, female may end up pregnant and then they live happily ever after. <br /><br />So, sorry Tiger. You don't get more than two stars. It's not you, it's the build up in the book. Please don't bite my head off.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16421325268319870317">Tiger, one of my favorite New Species, ran struggling down the mating aisle as soon as Zandy Gordon let him know she'd like to share sex. Zandy Gordon has had quite a bit of rough luck. Losing her job due to sexual harassment after two divorces has made it clear to her that she just cannot pick the right man to save her life.   <span id="freeText16421325268319870317" style="display:none">Tiger, one of my favorite New Species, ran struggling down the mating aisle as soon as Zandy Gordon let him know she'd like to share sex. Zandy Gordon has had quite a bit of rough luck. Losing her job due to sexual harassment after two divorces has made it clear to her that she just cannot pick the right man to save her life. While drowning her sorrows at a local bar, a fight breaks out and she needs to be rescued. Sure that her savior is a fallen angel she acts the wanton. But her savior is none other than confirmed bachelor and human female avoider, Tiger. <br /> <br />I really enjoyed this storyline as it gave insight to NSO headquarters while introducing more New Species (and a human worker) and placing a magnifying glass on how dedicated some of the hate groups are toward them. Excitement mounted as some of the hate groups mistook Zandy for Jessie and placed her in grave danger. Once again the literal and blunt language of the New Species provided fun in communications, much at Mandy's expense, and provided true laugh out loud moments for this reader. Zandy was a great heroine with her sass, sense of humor, insecurities and attitude. She and Tiger made a good couple. Tiger brought his "hole-ish" behavior out for a walk, but when he was good.... <br /><br />Originally Read: December 24, 2013<br />Rating: 4.75 Stars Actually<br />More reviews can be found at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.ireadthatbook.com">http://www.ireadthatbook.com</a><br /></span>

  <span id="freeText174402628074552265" style="display:none">3-1/2 stars. Parts of this I really liked and parts were annoying. Let me just state that I'm far from a prude but this book had about 7 back to back sex scenes. And those were only the back to back ones. They had sex 3 distinct times on their second encounter. Then the next morning she came back to work, they had a picnic and did it 4 more times. I just started thinking crap could you guys do something except boink like bunnies? It picked up in the second half when they started to have some actual time apart and some problems. The opening scene was nice also. I liked the crazy Vengenance character and hope he has a story coming. On the whole I enjoyed the book, I just don't like it when the sex overwhelms the plot.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('CHIqlaHWtCDsDrnkrUAEGOsqYpAtcI0FtjqkMat4AE2mvhL63930lbi+XMmABAbXH1mwuGfaLNpYF2McpU5Z3A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer14616671225793235601">I had a rather short area here telling a little about me but then I had more than a few people ask me to expand it so... here goes. LOL. I'm a full time home 'supervisor' which is a nice word for saying I'm a housewife. I'm married happily, I met my dream guy 20 years ago, and we have 4 children. I live in Southern California and I can't function without iced coffee. I believe in romance, I've alw</span>
  <span id="freeText14616671225793235601" style="display:none">I had a rather short area here telling a little about me but then I had more than a few people ask me to expand it so... here goes. LOL. I'm a full time home 'supervisor' which is a nice word for saying I'm a housewife. I'm married happily, I met my dream guy 20 years ago, and we have 4 children. I live in Southern California and I can't function without iced coffee. I believe in romance, I've always been a daydreamer, and I'm a HUGE fan of books, always have been.<br /><br />No, I didn't know that I always wanted to write. I inhaled books as a child. I read entire series (Pippi Longstocking, Nancy Drew and The Hardy Boys, Trixie Beldon, The Borrowers, etc) in a matter of days at a time. By the time I was nine years old I had an adult library card where I visited often. I moved on to John Saul, Stephen King, Richard Laymon, Agatha Christie, and then found romance. I was hooked. I wrote poetry in my teens and then moved on to short stories. My first book was started after I read a real bomb of a book that ticked me off with really horrible characters and a plot that was shabby at best and I thought... I could do better. LOL.<br /><br />I wrote my first book which will probably never see the light of day in the early 90's. I wrote a series of a few books from it. I'm a series fan! I kept writing for fun, wrote MANY books and then in 2009 I decided to try to get published. I wrote my first Sci Fi romance and Ral's Woman came to be. I submitted it and with a little tweaking, Ellorascave sent me an acceptance letter. It was kind of a 'Cinderella' experience for me. It's been a terrific ride so far and I'm really happy that I finally had the time to commit to writing full time. It's a dream come true.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14616671225793235601" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
